3.7.1 eywjqvb Dccv`Ļ (Boolean Theorems)

ewy jqvb Dccv`Ļi mvnvhĻ hywģ ivwkgvjvi mijxKiY ev ivwkgvjvi MVb cwieZĐb mvab Kiv hvq|

eywjqvb PjKi gvb Ô1Õ A_ev Ô0Õ w`q Gme Dccv`Ļļjv mnRB cÖgvY Kiv hvq| wbP ļiæZĄcY~ Đ

wKQz eywjqvb Dccv`Ļ `qv njv-

gSwjK Dccv`Ļ (Basic Theorems)                       5. mnvqK Dccv`Ļ (Auxiliary Theorems):
                                                    i) A + AB = A + B
1. i) A + 1 = 1                   ii) A .1= A       ii) A + AB = A + B
                                                    iii) A + AB = A + B
2. i) A + 0 = A                   ii) A .0 = 0      iv) A + AB = A + B

3. i) A + A = 1                   ii) A .A = 0

4. i) A + A = A                   ii) A .A = A

6. wewbgq Dccv`Ļ (Commulative Theorems)

     i) A + B = B + A             ii) A.B = B.A

7. Abyl― Dccv`Ļ (Associative Theorems)

     i) A + (B + C) = (A + B) + C ii) A .(B.C) = (A .B).C

8. wefvRb Dccv`Ļ (Distributed Theorems)

     i) A(B + C) = AB + AC ii) (A + B) (A + C) = A + BC

9. wW-giMĻvbi Dccv`Ļ (De-Morgan's Theorems)

     i) A + B = A.B               ii) A.B = A + B

10. mnvqK Dccv`Ļ (Secondary Theorems)

     i) A + AB = A                ii) A(A + B) = A

11. A = A

DcwiDģ Dccv`Ļmg~nK PjKi gvb 0 ev 1 ai hKvbv Dccv`Ļ cÖgvY Kiv hvq|

     long Factorial (int n)

     {

     if (n <=1)

        return 1;

     else

        return (n * Factorial (n-1));

     }
